[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[39mat [0m[1;35mcom.example.XliffParserFuzzer.parseOne[0m[1;39m([0m[39mXliffParserFuzzer.jav[0m[1;92ma:53[0m[1;39m)[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[39mat [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mcom.example.XliffParserFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m([0m[39mXliffParserFuzzer.jav[0m[1;92ma:40[0m[1;39m)[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDEDUP_TOKEN: b20b8002ee0350e2[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== libFuzzer crashing input ==[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Server Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m vulnerability has been detected in the Apache [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTika XLIFF12Parser component. The vulnerability was triggered during fuzzing and [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresulted in an attempted connection to an external domain [0m[1;39m([0m[39mjazze.com:[0m[1;36m80[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. This [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecurity issue is classified as medium severity and indicates that the parser can [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbe exploited to make unauthorized network requests based on untrusted XML input [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata.[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a Server Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m vulnerability, which allows an [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattacker to cause the application to make HTTP requests to arbitrary destinations. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAs noted in the exception message, [0m[32m"Requests to destinations based on untrusted [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mdata could lead to exfiltration of sensitive data or exposure of internal [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mservices."[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Issue Details[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability was detected by the Jazzer fuzzer's SSRF sanitizer when [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing XLIFF [0m[1;39m([0m[39mXML Localization Interchange File Format[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m files. The security [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcheck intercepted an attempted connection to [0m[32m"jazze.com:80"[0m[39m during XML parsing [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperations.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Stack Trace Analysis[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe stack trace reveals the following execution flow:[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The entry point is through `[0m[1;35mXliffParserFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` which calls [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mparseOne[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The parsing is initiated via `[0m[1;35mXLIFF12Parser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `[0m[1;35m_parse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` methods[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Standard Java XML SAX parsing infrastructure is invoked through [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mSAXParser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. The Xerces XML parser [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`XMLDocumentFragmentScannerImpl`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m processes the document[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. During entity reference scanning [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mscanEntityReference[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the parser attempts [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto resolve an external entity[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. The `XMLEntityManager` attempts to establish the actual entity by calling [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35msetupCurrentEntity[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. This triggers HTTP connection establishment through [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mHttpURLConnection.connect[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m8[0m[39m. The connection attempt is intercepted by the Jazzer SSRF sanitizer at the socket[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlevel[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Observations[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **External Entity Processing**: The vulnerability is triggered during XML entity[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreference scanning, suggesting that the XLIFF12Parser processes external entities [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefined in the XML content without proper validation or restrictions.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Network Connection Path**: The connection attempt goes through the standard [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJava HTTP client stack, indicating that the XML parser is configured to resolve [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal resources over the network.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Entity Manager Involvement**: The `[0m[1;35mXMLEntityManager.setupCurrentEntity[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mstartEntity[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` methods are directly involved in initiating the network request, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msuggesting that external entity resolution is enabled in the XML parser [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfiguration.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Document Fragment Scanning**: The vulnerability manifests during document [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfragment content processing, specifically when handling entity references within [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe XML document.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Areas to Investigate[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo obtain a holistic understanding of this vulnerability, the following components [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould be examined:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **XLIFF12Parser Configuration** [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`org.apache.tika.parser.xliff.XLIFF12Parser`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - How the SAXParser is configured and instantiated[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Whether external entity processing is explicitly enabled or disabled[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - What security features are configured for the XML parser[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `[0m[1;35m_parse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `[0m[1;35mparse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method implementations[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Parser Factory Settings**:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - SAXParserFactory configuration[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Features and properties set on the parser, particularly:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - `XMLConstants.FEATURE_SECURE_PROCESSING`[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - External entity resolution features[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - DTD processing features[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **XLIFF Specification Handling**:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Whether the XLIFF format specification requires external entity support[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - How the parser handles DOCTYPE declarations and entity definitions in XLIFF [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfiles[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Input Validation**:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If there are any allowlists or denylists for entity URIs[0m                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Related XLIFF Parsers**:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe SSRF vulnerability in XLIFF12Parser stems from the insecure `[0m[1;35m_parse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m78[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m89[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that creates a SAXParserFactory with only namespace awareness [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39menabled, lacking all security features to prevent external entity resolution. When [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe fuzzer provides XML with external entity references [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpointing to [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"jazze.com:80"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the parser attempts to resolve them over the network, triggering [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe SSRF vulnerability.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Vulnerable Code Pattern:**[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprivate static void [0m[1;35m_parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream is, DefaultHandler contentHandler, [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mParseContext context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    SAXParserFactory factory = [0m[1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mfactory.setNamespaceAware[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Only this - no security features[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    SAXParser parser = [0m[1;35mfactory.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mparser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, contentHandler[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Fix Implementation Steps[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Modify Imports in XLIFF12Parser.java[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Remove unsafe imports:**[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `javax.xml.parsers.ParserConfigurationException` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m24[0m[1;39m)[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `javax.xml.parsers.SAXParser` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m25[0m[1;39m)[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `javax.xml.parsers.SAXParserFactory` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m26[0m[1;39m)[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `org.xml.sax.helpers.DefaultHandler` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m31[0m[1;39m)[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Add secure import:**[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `org.apache.tika.utils.XMLReaderUtils`[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Remove the Vulnerable `[0m[1;35m_parse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` Method[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDelete the entire `[0m[1;35m_parse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m78[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m89[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m which creates the insecure [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSAXParser.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Update the `[0m[1;35mparse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` Method[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReplace the call to `[0m[1;35m_parse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in the `[0m[1;35mparse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m73[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m74[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with a direct [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcall to `[0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Replace:**[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35m_parse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mCloseShieldInputStream.wrap[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstream[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       new [0m[1;35mXLIFF12ContentHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mxhtml, metadata[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**With:**[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mCloseShieldInputStream.wrap[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstream[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                        new [0m[1;35mXLIFF12ContentHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mxhtml, metadata[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Why This Fix is Optimal[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Security Benefits[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix leverages the existing secure XML parsing infrastructure in Tika [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which provides multiple layers of security:[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **External Entity Blocking**: Disables `external-general-entities` and [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`external-parameter-entities` features[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **DTD Loading Prevention**: Disables `load-external-dtd` and `load-dtd-grammar` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfeatures[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Secure Processing**: Enables `XMLConstants.FEATURE_SECURE_PROCESSING`[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Entity Resolver**: Uses `IGNORING_SAX_ENTITY_RESOLVER` that returns empty [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstrings for all entity requests[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **OfflineContentHandler**: Wraps the ContentHandler to prevent network access at[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe handler level[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Xerces SecurityManager**: Limits entity expansion to prevent XML bomb attacks[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. **Parser Pooling**: Uses pre-configured secure parsers from a thread-safe pool[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Proven Pattern[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix follows the exact same pattern already used successfully in:[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **TMXParser** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m68[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Similar translation memory XML format parser[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **XMLParser base class** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m71[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: The standard secure XML parsing pattern in [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTika[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **DcXMLParser** and **FictionBookParser**: Both extend XMLParser for security[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Backward Compatibility[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix maintains complete backward compatibility:[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Same ContentHandler**: `XLIFF12ContentHandler` continues to receive identical [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSAX events[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Same Metadata**: All metadata extraction remains unchanged [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfile-count, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtu-count, languages[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Same Content**: Text extraction produces identical results[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Same Stream Handling**: `[0m[1;35mCloseShieldInputStream.wrap[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` usage is preserved[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Same ParseContext**: Context passing is maintained and properly utilized[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Test Compatibility**: All existing tests will pass because legitimate XLIFF [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfiles don't use external entities[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Why [0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Over Manual Configuration[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Option [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mRejected[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: Manually configure security features in `[0m[1;35m_parse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Requires maintaining duplicate security code[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Risk of missing security features[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No benefit from parser pooling[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Inconsistent with rest of Tika codebase[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Option [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mChosen[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: Use [0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ✓ Centralized security configuration[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ✓ Consistent with Tika's security architecture[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ✓ Proven effective [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtested in XMLReaderUtilsTest[0m[1;39m)[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ✓ Performance benefits from parser pooling[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ✓ Defense-in-depth with multiple security layers[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ✓ Minimal code changes[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ✓ Zero risk to existing functionality[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Why Not Extend XMLParser Base Class[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWhile extending XMLParser would also be secure, it's unnecessary because:[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- XLIFF12Parser has simple parsing requirements[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Direct use of [0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m matches the TMXParser pattern[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No need to override [0m[1;35mgetContentHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - XLIFF12ContentHandler is already custom[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Simpler change with less risk of breaking existing functionality[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- XLZParser depends on XLIFF12Parser's current structure[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Impact on Related Components[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### XLZParser [0m[1;39m([0m[39mNo Changes Required[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mXLZParser creates an instance of XLIFF12Parser [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m67[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and delegates parsing to [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mit. Once XLIFF12Parser is fixed, XLZParser automatically becomes secure without any[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodifications needed.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### XLIFF12ContentHandler [0m[1;39m([0m[39mNo Changes Required[0m[1;39m)[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe ContentHandler implementation extracts XLIFF-specific data [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtranslations, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmetadata[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and is designed to work with SAX events. It will receive identical events[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom the secure parser, so no changes are needed.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Existing Tests [0m[1;39m([0m[39mContinue Passing[0m[1;39m)[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix only changes the SAXParser security configuration, not the parsing logic. [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTests using legitimate XLIFF files [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwithout external entities[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will continue to [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpass because:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Standard XLIFF [0m[1;36m1.2[0m[39m files don't require external entity resolution[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The XLIFF specification doesn't mandate external DTD loading[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All inline content is processed identically[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m. Mitigation of Side Effects[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Potential Side Effect: External Schema References[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Concern**: XLIFF files with xsi:schemaLocation might fail if parser tries to [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidate[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Mitigation**: The secure configuration disables validation [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mfactory.setValidating[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfalse[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and only blocks external entity resolution in [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdocument content, not schema declarations used for namespace awareness. The test [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfile testXLIFF12.xlf already has `xsi:schemaLocation` and works correctly.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Potential Side Effect: Custom ParseContext SAXParser[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Concern**: Users providing custom SAXParser via ParseContext[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Mitigation**: [0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m properly checks ParseContext for custom [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSAXParser [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m522[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and uses it if provided, maintaining extensibility.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Potential Side Effect: Performance[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Concern**: Overhead from security features[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Mitigation**: Parser pooling actually improves performance by reusing configured [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsers. Security features have negligible overhead compared to parsing cost.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m. Verification[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix can be verified by:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Running existing XLIFF12ParserTest - should pass[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Testing with malicious XML containing external entities - should be blocked[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Fuzzing with the same input that triggered the SSRF - should not attempt network[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconnection[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Verifying XLZParser continues to work [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdelegates to fixed XLIFF12Parser[0m[1;39m)[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m. Summary[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix strategy:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ✓ Addresses the SSRF vulnerability by preventing external entity resolution[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ✓ Uses Tika's standard secure XML parsing infrastructure[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ✓ Maintains complete backward compatibility[0m                                       [2m                [0m
